vite.config.ts\n\n\u003c/project_structure\u003e\n\nOverview Content:\n\u003coverview_content\u003e\n\u003cblog\u003e\n# Comprehensive Project Analysis: Syrian Community Event Platform\n\n## 1. Project Introduction\n\nThis project appears to be a community event platform for the Syrian community, designed as a modern, multilingual web application. The application showcases event details with a focus on accessibility, internationalization, and responsive design.\n\n**Purpose Statement**:  \nTo provide a comprehensive digital platform for a Syrian community event, featuring event details, registration, agenda, speakers, and organizational information.\n\n**Core Goals and Objectives**:\n- Present event information in multiple languages (Arabic, English, Turkish)\n- Provide a responsive, accessible user interface\n- Showcase event components like agenda, speakers, and registration\n- Implement a modern, visually appealing design with Syrian cultural elements\n\n**Target Audience**:\n- Members of the Syrian diaspora community\n- Event organizers and participants\n- Multilingual users requiring RTL (right-to-left) language support\n- Mobile and desktop users seeking event information\n\n## 2. Technical Architecture\n\n### Component Breakdown\n\nThe application follows a modern React architecture with several key architectural decisions:\n\n- **Frontend Framework**: React 18 with TypeScript\n- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS with custom theme configuration\n- **Routing**: React Router DOM for client-side navigation\n- **State Management**: React Query for data fetching and caching\n- **UI Components**: ShadCN UI pattern with Radix UI primitives\n- **Build Tool**: Vite with React SWC plugin\n\n### Design Patterns\n\nThe project implements several modern design patterns:\n\n- **Component Composition**: Extensive use of reusable UI components\n- **Context API**: Language context for internationalization\n- **Custom Hooks**: Reusable logic encapsulation\n- **Atomic Design**: UI components organized in a design system pattern\n- **Theme Customization**: CSS variables with Tailwind theming\n\n### System Relationships\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n  A[Client Browser] --\u003e B[Vite Development Server]\n  B --\u003e C[React Application]\n  C --\u003e D[Tailwind CSS Styling]\n  C --\u003e E[React Router Navigation]\n  C --\u003e F[React Query Data Management]\n  C --\u003e G[Radix UI Primitives]\n  C --\u003e H[ShadCN Component Library]\n  C --\u003e I[Language Context]\n  D --\u003e J[Custom Theme Variables]\n  F --\u003e K[Event Data]\n```\n\n### Data Flow\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n  A[Client] --\u003e B[App Component]\n  B --\u003e C[LanguageProvider]\n  B --\u003e D[QueryClientProvider]\n  B --\u003e E[TooltipProvider]\n  C --\u003e F[useLanguage Hook]\n  B --\u003e G[BrowserRouter]\n  G --\u003e H[Routes]\n  H --\u003e I[Index Page]\n  I --\u003e J[Various Section Components]\n  J --\u003e K[UI Components]\n  K --\u003e L[Tailwind Styles]\n  F --\u003e M[Font Selection]\n  M --\u003e N[CSS Classes]\n```\n\n## 3. Key Implementation\n\n### Main Entry Points\n- `src/main.tsx` - Application entry point\n- `src/App.tsx` - Root application component\n- `src/pages/Index.tsx` - Main page component\n\n### Core Modules\n- `src/components/` - Reusable UI components\n- `src/data/eventData.ts` - Event data model\n- `src/hooks/` - Custom React hooks\n- `src/lib/utils.ts` - Utility functions\n\n### Configuration Approach\n- `vite.config.ts` - Vite build configuration\n- `tailwind.config.ts` - Tailwind CSS customization\n- `eslint.config.js` - Code linting rules\n- `package.json` - Dependencies and scripts\n\n### External Dependencies\n- React and React DOM\n- React Router DOM for routing\n- React Query for data management\n- Tailwind CSS for styling\n- ShadCN UI components built on Radix UI\n- Internationalization support\n\n### Integration Points\n- Custom font integration (Bahij Koufiya, Roboto)\n- Syrian color palette in theme\n- RTL language support\n- Responsive design for mobile\n\n### Component Relationships\n\n```mermaid\ngraph LR\n  App[App Component] --\u003e LanguageProvider[LanguageProvider]\n  App --\u003e QueryClientProvider[QueryClientProvider]\n  App --\u003e TooltipProvider[TooltipProvider]\n  App --\u003e BrowserRouter[BrowserRouter]\n  BrowserRouter --\u003e Routes[Routes]\n  Routes --\u003e Index[Index Page]\n  Routes --\u003e NotFound[NotFound Page]\n  Index --\u003e HeroSection[HeroSection]\n  Index --\u003e CountdownTimer[CountdownTimer]\n  Index --\u003e DetailsSection[DetailsSection]\n  Index --\u003e AgendaSection[AgendaSection]\n  Index --\u003e SpeakersSection[SpeakersSection]\n  Index --\u003e GoalsSection[GoalsSection]\n  Index --\u003e WhySection[WhySection]\n  Index --\u003e OrganizersSection[OrganizersSection]\n  Index --\u003e RegistrationSection[RegistrationSection]\n  Index --\u003e Footer[Footer]\n  HeroSection --\u003e Navbar[Navbar]\n  Navbar --\u003e LanguageSwitcher[LanguageSwitcher]\n  Navbar --\u003e NavLink[NavLink]\n  AllSections --\u003e UIComponents[UI Components]\n  UIComponents --\u003e Button[Button]\n  UIComponents --\u003e Card[Card]\n  UIComponents --\u003e Badge[Badge]\n  UIComponents --\u003e Avatar[Avatar]\n```\n\n## 4. Key Features\n\n### Functionality Overview\n\nThe application provides a comprehensive event website with the following features:\n\n- **Multilingual Support**: Arabic (RTL), English, and Turkish language options\n- **Responsive Design**: Mobile-first approach with adaptive layouts\n- **Event Countdown Timer**: Visual countdown to the event\n- **Comprehensive Event Information**: Agenda, ShadCN component library implementation\n- **Performance Optimization**: Vite build tool with code splitting\n- **Type Safety**: Full TypeScript implementation\n\n### Feature Architecture\n\n```mermaid\nstateDiagram-v2\n  [*] --\u003e Initial\n  Initial --\u003e LanguageSelection: App Load\n  LanguageSelection --\u003e ThemeApplication: Set Language\n  ThemeApplication
